\"FilterManager::decodeData\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"HTTP filter chain registration and execution in Envoy involves multiple layers of abstraction that separate configuration-time decisions from runtime behavior.\\n\\n## Registration Phase (Configuration Time)\\n\\nAt startup, the HttpConnectionManagerFilterConfigFactory (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.cc and config.h) creates an HttpConnectionManagerConfig instance when the HTTP connection manager filter is instantiated. The proto configuration is defined in envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto, which specifies an array of HttpFilter messages in the http_filters field.\\n\\nDuring HttpConnectionManagerConfig construction, a FilterChainHelper template class (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h) is instantiated to process the proto-defined filters. The FilterChainHelper::processFilters() method iterates through each HttpFilter in the configuration, validates it, and creates a FilterFactoryCb (a function pointer defined in envoy/http/filter_factory.h) for each filter. These factory callbacks are stored in the filter_factories_ list on the HttpConnectionManagerConfig.\\n\\nThe FilterChainFactory interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h) defines two key methods: createFilterChain() for normal streams and createUpgradeFilterChain() for WebSocket/upgrade requests. HttpConnectionManagerConfig implements this interface.\\n\\n## Execution Phase (Runtime)\\n\\nWhen a new HTTP stream arrives, the FilterManager (source/common/http/filter_manager.h) is created to manage that stream. The FilterManager also implements the FilterChainManager interface and contains the core iteration logic for executing filters.\\n\\nUpon the first request event (typically decoding headers), FilterManager::createFilterChain() is called. This method calls filter_chain_factory_.createFilterChain(), passing itself as the FilterChainManager implementation. HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain() then delegates to FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories() (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.cc).\\n\\nFilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories() iterates through the filter_factories_ list and for each enabled filter, calls manager.applyFilterFactoryCb(). This is a key integration point where the stored factory callbacks are executed.\\n\\nFilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb() (source/common/http/filter_manager.cc) creates a FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl instance, which implements the FilterChainFactoryCallbacks interface (envoy/http/filter.h). The factory callback is then invoked with this callbacks object. The factory function calls methods on FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl to register filters:\\n- addStreamDecoderFilter() for request path filters\\n- addStreamEncoderFilter() for response path filters  \\n- addStreamFilter() for bidirectional filters\\n\\nFilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl wraps these filters in ActiveStreamDecoderFilter and ActiveStreamEncoderFilter wrappers, which track iteration state and match data. These are added to FilterManager's decoder_filters_ and encoder_filters_ linked lists.\\n\\n## Filter Chain Iteration\\n\\nOnce filters are registered, FilterManager controls execution through methods like decodeHeaders(), decodeData(), encodeHeaders(), and encodeData(). Each method iterates through the appropriate filter list, calling the corresponding virtual methods on each filter and handling return status codes that control whether to continue, stop, or buffer data.\\n\\nThe key architectural pattern is the separation between:\\n1. FilterChainFactory - defines what filters to create\\n2. FilterChainFactoryCallbacks - provides the interface for filters to register themselves\\n3. runtime behavior.\\n\\n## Registration Phase (Configuration Time)\\n\\nAt startup, the HttpConnectionManagerFilterConfigFactory (source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.cc and config.h) creates an HttpConnectionManagerConfig instance when the HTTP connection manager filter is instantiated. The proto configuration is defined in envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto, which specifies an array of HttpFilter messages in the http_filters field.\\n\\nDuring HttpConnectionManagerConfig construction, a FilterChainHelper template class (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h) is instantiated to process the proto-defined filters. The FilterChainHelper::processFilters() method iterates through each HttpFilter in the configuration, validates it, and creates a FilterFactoryCb (a function pointer defined in envoy/http/filter_factory.h) for each filter. These factory callbacks are stored in the filter_factories_ list on the HttpConnectionManagerConfig.\\n\\nThe FilterChainFactory interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h) defines two key methods: createFilterChain() for normal streams and createUpgradeFilterChain() for WebSocket/upgrade requests. HttpConnectionManagerConfig implements this interface.\\n\\n## Execution Phase (Runtime)\\n\\nWhen a new HTTP stream arrives, the FilterManager (source/common/http/filter_manager.h) is created to manage that stream. The FilterManager also implements the FilterChainManager interface and contains the core iteration logic for executing filters.\\n\\nUpon the first request event (typically decoding headers), FilterManager::createFilterChain() is called. This method calls filter_chain_factory_.createFilterChain(), passing itself as the FilterChainManager implementation. HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain() then delegates to FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories() (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.cc).\\n\\nFilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories() iterates through the filter_factories_ list and for each enabled filter, calls manager.applyFilterFactoryCb(). This is a key integration point where the stored factory callbacks are executed.\\n\\nFilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb() (source/common/http/filter_manager.cc) creates a FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl instance, which implements the FilterChainFactoryCallbacks interface (envoy/http/filter.h). The factory callback is then invoked with this callbacks object. The factory function calls methods on FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl to register filters:\\n- addStreamDecoderFilter() for request path filters\\n- addStreamEncoderFilter() for response path filters  \\n- addStreamFilter() for bidirectional filters\\n\\nFilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl wraps these filters in ActiveStreamDecoderFilter and ActiveStreamEncoderFilter wrappers, which track iteration state and match data. These are added to FilterManager's decoder_filters_ and encoder_filters_ linked lists.\\n\\n## Filter Chain Iteration\\n\\nOnce filters are registered, FilterManager controls execution through methods like decodeHeaders(), decodeData(), encodeHeaders(), and encodeData(). Each method iterates through the appropriate filter list, calling the corresponding virtual methods on each filter and handling return status codes that control whether to continue, stop, or buffer data.\\n\\nThe key architectural pattern is the separation between:\\n1. FilterChainFactory - defines what filters to create\\n2. FilterChainFactoryCallbacks - provides the interface for filters to register themselves\\n3. FilterManager - implements both FilterChainManager (receives registrations) and controls runtime iteration\\n4. FilterChainUtility - bridges configuration-time factories with runtime instantiation\\n\\nThis design allows Envoy to support dynamic filter configuration through ECDS (Extension Configuration Discovery Service) while maintaining strict ordering and dependency management through the DependencyManager.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
